        alert = function () { };

        var agenciesList = "";
        var locationsList = "";
        var listItems = "";
        var CategoryListItems = "";
        var selectAllOptions = "";

        var sacl = $('#selectAllCatLoc').val();
        if (sacl !== "true") { sacl = false; } else { sacl = true; }

        // Set to true, if all categories and locations should be selected by default upon selecting an agency, otherwise false
        selectAllOptions = selectAll(sacl);

        //GetAgencies();
        //GetLocations();

        function PopulateAgencyListItems() {
            var AgencyListItems = "";
            for (var i = 0; i < agenciesList.length; i++) {
                AgencyListItems += "<option value='" + agenciesList[i].code + "'>" + agenciesList[i].name + "</option>";
            }

            $('select#agencySelectionBox').html(AgencyListItems);
            var select = $('select#agencySelectionBox');
            select.html(select.find('option').sort(function (x, y) {
                // to change to descending order switch "<" for ">"
                return $(x).text() > $(y).text() ? 1 : -1;
            }));
            $('select#agencySelectionBox').selectpicker('refresh');
        }

        // Update Location Dropdown
        var updateSelectLocationBox = function (category) {
            if (category) {
                for (var i = 0; i < locationsList.length; i++) {
                    if (!$('select#agencySelectionBox').val()) {
                        if (category) {
                            if (category === locationsList[i].category) {
                                listItems += "<option " + selectAllOptions + " value='" + locationsList[i].name + "'>" + locationsList[i].name + "-" + locationsList[i].agencyabbr + "</option>";
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (category.toString().split('-')[0] === locationsList[i].category && category.toString().split('-')[1] === locationsList[i].agencyabbr) {
                            listItems += "<option " + selectAllOptions + " value='" + locationsList[i].name + "'>" + locationsList[i].name + "-" + locationsList[i].agencyabbr + "</option>";
                        }
                        if ($('select#agencySelectionBox').val()) {
                            var agencyFound = $('select#agencySelectionBox').val().toString().split(',');
                            var isAgencyFound = agencyFound.indexOf(locationsList[i].agencyabbr);
                        } 
                        else {
                            var isAgencyFound = -1;
                        }
                        if (category === locationsList[i].category && (isAgencyFound != -1)) {
                            listItems += "<option " + selectAllOptions + " value='" + locationsList[i].name + "'>" + locationsList[i].name + "-" + locationsList[i].agencyabbr + "</option>";
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            $('select#locationSelectionBox').html(listItems);
            var select = $('select#locationSelectionBox');
            select.html(select.find('option').sort(function (x, y) {
                // to change to descending order switch "<" for ">"
                return $(x).text() > $(y).text() ? 1 : -1;
            }));
            $('select#locationSelectionBox').selectpicker('refresh');
        }

        // Update Category Dropdown
        var updateSelectCategoryBox = function (agency) {
            var agencyListItemsNoOption = "";
            for (var i = 0; i < locationsList.length; i++) {
                if (agency === "all") {
                    agencyListItemsNoOption += locationsList[i].category + ',';
                }
                else {
                    if (agency === locationsList[i].agencyabbr) {
                        agencyListItemsNoOption += locationsList[i].category + '-' + locationsList[i].agencyabbr + ',';
                    }
                }
            }

            agencyListItemsNoOption = agencyListItemsNoOption.substring(0, agencyListItemsNoOption.length - 1);
            agencyListItemsNoOption = cleanCSV(agencyListItemsNoOption);

            if (agencyListItemsNoOption !== null) {
                var selectedCategories = agencyListItemsNoOption.toString().split(',');
                for (var i = 0; i < selectedCategories.length; i++) {
                    var agencyCode = selectedCategories[i].toString().split('-')[1];
                    if (wordInString(CategoryListItems, selectedCategories[i].toString().split('-')[0]) == false) {
                        if (agency !== "all" && agency === agencyCode) {
                            CategoryListItems += "<option " + selectAllOptions + " value='" + selectedCategories[i].toString().split('-')[0] + "'>" + selectedCategories[i].toString().split('-')[0] + "</option>";
                            if (selectAllOptions === "selected") { updateSelectLocationBox(selectedCategories[i]); }
                        }
                        else {
                            CategoryListItems += "<option value='" + selectedCategories[i].toString().split('-')[0] + "'>" + selectedCategories[i].toString().split('-')[0] + "</option>";
                            //if (selectAllOptions === "selected") { updateSelectLocationBox(selectedCategories[i]); }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            $('select#categorySelectionBox').html(CategoryListItems);
            var select = $('select#categorySelectionBox');
            select.html(select.find('option').sort(function (x, y) {
                // to change to descending order switch "<" for ">"
                return $(x).text() > $(y).text() ? 1 : -1;
            }));           
            $('select#categorySelectionBox').selectpicker('refresh');
        }

        if ($('select#agencySelectionBox').val() == "") {
            //nothing selected;
            updateSelectCategoryBox("all");
        }

        // Agency change
        $('select#agencySelectionBox').on('change', function () {
            CategoryListItems = "";
            if (!$('select#agencySelectionBox').val()) {
                //nothing selected;
                updateSelectCategoryBox("all");
            }
            else {
                //something selected;
                var selectedValue = $('select#agencySelectionBox').val();
                if (selectedValue !== null) {
                    var selectedAgencies = selectedValue.toString().split(',');
                    for (i = 0; i < selectedAgencies.length; i++) {
                        updateSelectCategoryBox(selectedAgencies[i]);
                    }
                }
            }
            $('select#categorySelectionBox').trigger('change', true);
            DeleteAllMarkers();
            CreateMarker();
        });

        // Category change
        $('select#categorySelectionBox').on('change', function () {
            listItems = "";
            var selectedValue = $('select#categorySelectionBox').val();
            if (selectedValue !== null) {
                var selectedCategories = selectedValue.toString().split(',');
                for (i = 0; i < selectedCategories.length; i++) {
                    updateSelectLocationBox(selectedCategories[i]);
                }
            }
            $('select#locationSelectionBox').trigger('change', true);
            DeleteAllMarkers();
            CreateMarker();
        });

        // Location change
        $('select#locationSelectionBox').on('change', function () {
            $('select#locationSelectionBox').html(listItems);
            var select = $('select#locationSelectionBox');
            select.html(select.find('option').sort(function (x, y) {
                // to change to descending order switch "<" for ">"
                return $(x).text() > $(y).text() ? 1 : -1;
            }));
            $('select#locationSelectionBox').selectpicker('refresh');
            DeleteAllMarkers();
            CreateMarker();
        });


        // Map initialization
        var map;
        var marker;
        var markerArr = [];

        var myOptions = {
            center: new google.maps.LatLng(31.3113, -92.4451),  // Alexandria, LA           //(locationsList[0].latitude, locationsList[0].longitude),
            zoom: 7,
            mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP,
            styles: [
                {
                    featureType: "poi.business",
                    elementType: "labels",
                    stylers: [
                        { visibility: "off" }
                    ]
                }
            ]
        };
        map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('map'), myOptions);

        // Define the marker icons
        var iconBase = document.location.protocol + '//' + document.location.host + '/Content/images/';

        var icons = {
            parking: {
                icon: iconBase + 'parking_lot_maps.png'
            },

        // Create Marker(s)
        function CreateMarker() {
            var selectedValue = $('select#locationSelectionBox').val();
            if (selectedValue !== null) {

                var selectedLocations = selectedValue.toString().split(',');
                for (var i = 0; i <= locationsList.length - 1; i++) {
                    var ltlng = [];
                    var markerIcon = "";

                    if (selectedLocations.indexOf(locationsList[i].name) !== -1) {
                        ltlng.push(new google.maps.LatLng(locationsList[i].latitude, locationsList[i].longitude));

                        markerIcon = GetMarkerIcon("default");  //GetMarkerIcon(locationsList[i].category);

                        marker = new google.maps.Marker({
                            map: map,
                            animation: google.maps.Animation.DROP,
                            icon: markerIcon,
                            title: locationsList[i].agency,
                            position: ltlng[0]
                        });
                        // Save markers
                        markerArr.push(marker);

                        (function (marker, i) {
                            google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function () {
                                var locationAddr1 = "";
                                var locationAddr2 = "";
                                var website = "";
                                //
                                var phoneNum = locationsList[i].phone.replace(/\-/g, '.');  // Replace all dashes with period
                                phoneNum = phoneNum.replace(/\(/g, ' ');                    // Replace all left parens with space
                                phoneNum = phoneNum.replace(/\)/g, '.');                    // Replace all right parens with period
                                phoneNum = phoneNum.replace(/\ /g, '');                     // Replace all spaces with null
                                //
                                if (locationsList[i].website.substring(0, 4) === "http") { website = locationsList[i].website.substring(7); }
                                if (locationsList[i].website.substring(0, 5) === "https") { website = locationsList[i].website.substring(12); }
                                if (website.substring(website.length - 1) === "/") { website = website.substring(0, website.length - 1); }
                                //
                                if (locationsList[i]["address 1"] === undefined) {
                                    locationAddr1 = locationsList[i]["address1"];
                                }
                                else {
                                    locationAddr1 = locationsList[i]["address 1"];
                                }
                                if (locationsList[i]["address 2"] === undefined) {
                                    locationAddr2 = locationsList[i]["address2"];
                                }
                                else {
                                    locationAddr2 = locationsList[i]["address 2"];
                                }
                                //
                                var infowindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow({ maxWidth: 250 });
                                infowindow.setContent('<strong>' + locationsList[i].name + '<br>' + locationsList[i].agency + '<br>' + locationAddr1 + '<br>' + locationAddr2 + '<br>' + locationsList[i].city + ', ' + locationsList[i].state + ' ' + locationsList[i].zip + '<br>' + locationsList[i].category + '<br>' + phoneNum + '<br><a target="_blank" href="' + locationsList[i].website + '">' + website + '</a></strong>');
                                infowindow.open(map, marker);
                            });

                        })(marker, i);
                    }
                }
            }
        };

        // Remove All Markers
        function DeleteAllMarkers() {
            for (var i = 0; i < markerArr.length; i++) {
                markerArr[i].setMap(null);
            }
            return;
        }

        // Get Marker Icon
        function GetMarkerIcon(category) {
            var mi = "";

            switch (category) {
                case 'Office':
                    mi = icons['office'].icon;
                    break;
                default:
                    mi = icons['spotLight'].icon;
            }
            return mi;
        }

        // Clean up duplicates
        function cleanCSV(value) {
            return (value || '').split(',').filter(Boolean).filter(function (item, index, all) {
                return (index === all.indexOf(item));
            });
        }

        // Select ALL options for category and location dropdowns
        function selectAll(selected) {
            if (selected) {
                return selectedAttrib = "selected";
            }
            else {
                return selectedAttrib = "";
            }
        }

        function wordInString(s, word) {
            return new RegExp('\\b' + word + '\\b', 'i').test(s);
        }

        function CapitalizeWords(str) {
            return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, function (txt) { return txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase(); });
        }

        //
        // AJAX : Agencies and Locations
        //
        function GetAgencies() {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: $('#agenciesUrl').val(),
                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                async: true,
                xhrFields: {
                    // The 'xhrFields' property sets additional fields on the XMLHttpRequest.
                    // This can be used to set the 'withCredentials' property.
                    // Set the value to 'true' if you'd like to pass cookies to the server.
                    // If this is enabled, your server must respond with the header
                    // 'Access-Control-Allow-Credentials: true'.
                    withCredentials: false
                },
                beforeSend: function (xhr) {
                    xhr.setRequestHeader("x-api-key", $('#dataApiKey').val());
                },
                success: function (data) {
                    agenciesList = data;
                    PopulateAgencyListItems();
                    GetLocations();
                },
                error: function (result) {
                    alert("Error: " + JSON.stringify(result));
                }
            });
        }

        function GetLocations() {
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: $('#locationsUrl').val(),
                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                async: true,
                xhrFields: {
                    // The 'xhrFields' property sets additional fields on the XMLHttpRequest.
                    // This can be used to set the 'withCredentials' property.
                    // Set the value to 'true' if you'd like to pass cookies to the server.
                    // If this is enabled, your server must respond with the header
                    // 'Access-Control-Allow-Credentials: true'.
                    withCredentials: false
                },
                beforeSend: function (xhr) {
                    xhr.setRequestHeader("x-api-key", $('#dataApiKey').val());
                },
                success: function (data) {
                    locationsList = data;
                    updateSelectCategoryBox("all");
                    CreateMarker();
                },
                error: function (result) {
                    alert("Error: " + JSON.stringify(result));
                }
            });
        }

        // No longer needed at this time
        //$('.filter-option-inner-inner').eq(0).text('-FIRST SELECTION-');

        // Load the map
        google.maps.event.addDomListener(window, 'load', GetAgencies());
    });

</script>

            <div class="container-fluid my-2" style="padding: 10px;"> 
             <div class="row pt-2"> 
              <div class="pagination-container"> 
               <!--<nav class="mr-2">
            				<ul class="pagination">
            					
            				</ul>
            
            			</nav>--> 
              </div> 
              <div class="form-group col input-group-sm"></div> 
              <div class="rows_count col float-right text-right"></div>

         <script>
    function getPagination(paginationId, maxRows) {
        let paginationDiv = $('#' + paginationId);
        let totalRows = 0;

        $('.pagination-container', paginationDiv).html(''); 
        $('.ost', paginationDiv).each(function() { 
            let me = $(this);
            me.removeAttr('data-page-number');
            if (me.css('display') !== 'none') {
                totalRows++;
                me.attr('data-page-number', Math.ceil(totalRows / maxRows));
            }
        });
        
        let pagenum = Math.ceil(totalRows / maxRows);
      
        $('.tempItems').remove();
        paginationDiv.append('<input type="hidden" class="maxPageNum tempItems" value="' + pagenum + '" />')
            .append('<input type="hidden" class="currentPageNum tempItems" value="1" />');
        
        if (pagenum > 0) {
            let paginationElement = $('.pagination-container', paginationDiv);
           
            paginationElement.append('<div class="pagination">'+
            '<button type="button" data-page="previous" class="page-item"><span><i class="fas fa-angle-left"></i></span></button>'+
            '<input class="paginationNumber" type="text" size="4" style="line-height:34px; text-align:center; font-size:18px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:2px;">'+
            '<label class="" style="font-size:17px;">&nbsp;of ' + pagenum + '</label>'+
            '<button type="button" data-page="next" class="page-item"><span><i class="fas fa-angle-right"></i></span></button>'+ 
            '</div>').show();
        
            $('.paginationNumber', paginationDiv).off('keyup').on('keyup', function(e) {
                let c = $('.currentPageNum', paginationDiv);
                let me = $(this);
                let max = parseInt($('.maxPageNum', paginationDiv).val());
                if (me.val() !== '') {
                    if (/^\d+$/.test(me.val())) {
                        let num = parseInt(me.val());
                        showPage(num <= max ? num : c.val(), paginationDiv, c);
                    } else {
                        showPage(c.val(), paginationDiv, c);
                    }
                }
            }).off('blur').on('blur', function() {
                let me = $(this);
                if (me.val() === '') {
                    me.val($('.currentPageNum', paginationDiv).val());
                }
                $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
            });
        
            $('.pagination button', paginationDiv).off().on('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                
                let attrValue = $(this).attr('data-page');
                let current = $('.currentPageNum', paginationDiv);
                let max = $('.maxPageNum', paginationDiv);
                let shouldProcess = true;
                
                if (attrValue === 'previous') {
                    if (current.val() === '1') {
                        shouldProcess = false;
                    } else {
                        attrValue = parseInt(current.val()) - 1;
                    }
                }
                else if (attrValue === 'next') {
                    if (max.val() !== current.val()) {
                        attrValue = parseInt(current.val()) + 1;
                    } else {
                        shouldProcess = false;
                    }
                } 
                
                if (shouldProcess) {
                    showPage(attrValue, paginationDiv, current);
                    $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
                }
            });
        }
    }
    
    function showPage(pageNumber, paginationDiv, current) {
        if (isNaN(pageNumber)) {
            return;
        }
        let paginationNumber = $('.paginationNumber', paginationDiv);
        
        paginationNumber.val(pageNumber);
        current.val(pageNumber);
        let newValue = parseInt(pageNumber);
        $("[data-page-number]", paginationDiv).each(function (i, v) {
            let value = $(v);
            if (parseInt(value.attr('data-page-number')) === newValue) {
                value.show()
            } else {
                value.hide();
            }
        });
    }
    
    function showFirstPage(paginationId) {
        let paginationDiv = $('#' + paginationId);
        showPage(1, paginationDiv, $('.currentPageNum', paginationDiv));
    }
</script> 
        </section> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="modal-footer"> 
      <button type="button" class="btn btn-secondary" data-dismiss="modal">Close</button> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </div> 
  </div>

  <!-- Start of Search code --> 
  <script>
    var googleSearchButton;
    var googleSearchText;
    var items;
    var laGovSearch;
    var modalSearch;
    var myModal;
    var onlineServicesCount;
    var timer = null;
    
    $(function() {
        modalSearch = $('#modalSearch');
        myModal = $('#myModal');
        onlineServicesCount = $('#online-services-count');
        items = $('.ost', myModal);
        
        $('.relatedButtons', myModal).hide();
        
        $('.custom-service-title', myModal).removeClass().addClass('col-md-12 col-sm-12 p-3');
        $('.custom-service-body', myModal).removeClass().addClass('col-md-12 col-sm-12 p-3 ml-auto');
        
        onlineServicesCount.text(items.length.toString() + (items.length > 1 ? ' Online Services' : 'Online Service'));
        laGovSearch = $('#laGovSearch');
        
        laGovSearch.on('keyup', function(e) {
            if (e.keyCode != 27) {
                clearTimeout(timer);
                if (laGovSearch.val().length >= 3) {
                    myModal.modal('show');
                    modalSearch.focus().val(laGovSearch.val());
                }
            }
        });
        
        modalSearch.on('keyup', function() {
            clearTimeout(timer);
            if (modalSearch.val().length >= 3) {
                timer = setTimeout(keywordSearch, 500);
            }
        });
        
        myModal.on("hidden.bs.modal", function () {
            laGovSearch.val('');
        });
    });

    function keywordSearch() {
        let count = 0;
        let keywords = modalSearch.val();
        items.each(function (index, value) {
            let me = $(this);
            let wasFound = false;
    
            $(value).find('.searchText').each(function (j) {
                let currentDiv = me[0];
                if (currentDiv.innerText.toLowerCase().indexOf(keywords) >= 0) {
                    wasFound = true;
                    return false;
                }
            });
            if (wasFound) {
                me.show();
                count++;
            }
            else {
                me.hide();
            }
        });
        onlineServicesCount.text(count.toString() + (count === 1 ? ' Online Service' : ' Online Services'));
        getPagination('result', 10);
        showFirstPage('result');
        instance.execute(keywords);
    }

(function($){
    $.fn.setCursorToTextEnd = function() {
        var $initialVal = this.val();
        this.val($initialVal);
    };
})(jQuery);

</script>

  <script>
    var instance = null;
    var customSearchControl = null;
    var myCallback = function() {
        if (document.readyState == 'complete') {
            // Document is ready when CSE element is initialized.
            // Render an element with both search box and search results in div with id 'cse_g'.
            instance = google.search.cse.element.render(
            {
                div: "cse_g",
                tag: 'search',
                gname: 'cse_g',
                attributes: {
                    noResultsString: "No Results",
                    overlayResults: false
                }
            });
        } else {
            // Document is not ready yet, when CSE element is initialized.
            google.setOnLoadCallback(function() {
                // Render an element with both search box and search results in div with id 'test'.
                instance = google.search.cse.element.render(
                {
                    div: "cse_g",
                    tag: 'searchresults-only',
                    gname: 'cse_g',
                    attributes: {
                        noResultsString: "No Results",
                        overlayResults: false
                    }
                });
            }, true);
        }
    };
    
    // Insert it before the CSE code snippet so that cse.js can take the script
    // parameters, like parsetags, callbacks.
    window.__gcse = {
        parsetags: 'explicit',
        callback: myCallback
    };
    
    (function() {
        var cx = '016838695848455624926:8a1zl511ibc'; // Custom Search engine ID 
        var gcse = document.createElement('script'); 
        gcse.type = 'text/javascript';
        gcse.async = true;
        gcse.src = 'https://cse.google.com/cse.js?cx=' + cx;
        var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(gcse, s);
    })();
</script>
